1065 : Ad 53.28 |Ad 53.28: hinaturan ta sira sandhyāśoca saha widhiwidhāna liniku-likuran. Hooykaas, Hinduism of Bali: ``it is used on the occasion of the grinding of the bones of the incinerated body, asthi-widhāna, but also at ṅarorasin (12 days after incineration), linikur-likuran (at least 21 days after it), ligia / bukur (at least 42 days after) and luwĕr (long after it, incineration is a potlatch, the others are bigger)''.  likur I
